< Review>
I reserved a space by phone in April, I was moving from Virginia to Torrance, Calif.     Robin helped me set up the transition she was very helpful. Gave me a competitive price for 3 months of 99.00 monthly, I went in the office on the 14th of May to pay for the first month but when I arrived I found out there was also a 20.00 administration charge that I was not told about and the prorated amount I had to pay for the 17 days I had left in the month of may was not calculated by the amount I was paying a month, it was considerably more but I paid it.  My boxes arrived the 19th and I moved my stuff in and realized I could use a smaller size it was less than 1/2 full so I  asked about downsizing was told no problem but the price was only 17.00 less a month than what I was paying for double the size. I was hoping she would understand the situation and work with me. I have rented storage spaces before and they always work with you because they want your business and am sure want you to be happy you are a customer there and not somewhere else. but no she was not going to help this situation at all. I thought about it for a few days. Then paid my rent for June and went back  in  deciding to go ahead and change sizes  we started the paperwork and then she told me I would have to pay another 20.00 administration fee for the different unit.....give me a break! I had only been there for just over 2 weeks all the info was the same. That was it, I said no thank you and  I went to my storage unit and loaded my car, with 2 trips I was out (see that's how little boxes I had they all fit into my Honda civic). I'm sorry I would not recommend this place to anyone unless you have no mind to spending any amount of money. If you are on a budget don't bother.< /Review>

Pretty cool pub. Set-up is a little disjointed, with two bar areas otherwise joined at the hip, but different atmospheres. Music rocks, a lot of classic rock if you're into that.

Their happy hour needs revising, instead of having half price drinks they have 2 for 1 drinks....this is not the same guys. This is absolutely not good if you either have an odd number of guests, or 1 guest - reason:  it just promotes fast drinking as staff open/pour the two drinks at the same time [beer for instance], so obviously you don't want it to go flat. Better just to make it half price for one.</Review>
